<script>

	aosDomain = "https://id.rlcdn.com/387146.gif?partner_uid"; // Global variable for the liveramp BAU Url - CSI
	peOfferServiceThrottle = true; // Boolean value for throttling of users for SSI Vs CSI
	var isPeOfferSSIServiceFlag = ""; // String value for the forced integration users
	var peOfferServiceThrottleValue = "100", // String value for the percentage of users throttled for SSI 
		liveRampUrl_NGA = "https://id.rlcdn.com/463166.gif?partner_uid"; // Global value for the live Ramp SSI Url - Prior to Oct 2018

	// PE Citi.com Liveramp Call function - New api domain - Oct 2018
	
	var liveRampFeatureOct18 = true, // Global variable for the liveramp integration feature - Oct 2018 release
		liveRampUrl_CSI_Oct18 = "https://di.rlcdn.com/387146.gif?partner_uid", // Global variable for the liveRamp old api CSI - Oct 2018
		liveRampUrl_SSI_Oct18 = "https://di.rlcdn.com/463166.gif?partner_uid", // Global variable for the new liveRamp old api SSI - Oct 2018
		liveRampUrl_newApi_Oct18 = "https://api.rlcdn.com/api/identity", // Global variable for the new liveRamp api - Oct 2018
		liveRampTimeout_newApi_Oct18 = "700", // Global variable for the new liveRamp api time out value - Oct 2018
		liveRampStatus = {
				"success" : "", // Node to store the success state of the Live Ramp new api integration and node in format - Success message|idl_value
				"failure" : "" // Node to store the failure/exception messages for the Live Ramp new api integration
		},
		idl = "", // Initiate the Live Ramp idl value to empty string for later use
		vendorData = {
               "acxiom_gpol": {
                              "payloadSize": 16384,
                              "AOSSuccessRCode": "I000",
                              "AOSMetaData": "[^-|{:},.\\t\\n\\r [\\]\"A-Za-z0-9_]",
                              "blackListKeywords": ["script", "embed", "object"],
                              "whiteListVariables": ["GPOLRs", "rCode", "rMsg", "ofrlst", "attributes", "mem", "name", "value", "type", "rank", "mcode", "scode", "brd", "pid","uc", "csec", "fr", "lvl", "c", "pl","spl","m", "axDP", "axDS", "axIPO", "axCan", "src", "ecm", "rvw", "cmp", "brk", "ret", "bk", "pgid", "uid", "pd", "subc","spd","rvd","tad", "cat","ep","pr","mr", "bpr", "cmv", "rpr"]
               },
               "RF": {
                              "payloadSize": 16384,
                              "RFMetaData": "[^-|{:},.?\\t\\n\\r [\\]\"A-Za-z0-9_~=/&^]",
        "blackListKeywords": ["script","embed","object"],
        "whiteListVariables": [ "rf_placement1","rf_placement2","rf_placement3","rf_placement4","rf_placement5","rf_placement6","rf_placement7","rf_placement8","pid","contentID","moduletype","decisionType","clickURL","scenarioID","creativeGroupID","creativename","rf_placements","rf_bannerService","templateID"]
               },
               "OS": {
                              "payloadSize": 16384,
                              "OSMetaData": "[^-|{:},.?\\t\\n\\r [\\]\"A-Za-z0-9_~=/&^]",
                              "blackListKeywords": ["script", "embed", "object"],
                              "whiteListVariables": [ "rf_placement1","rf_placement2","rf_placement3","rf_placement4","rf_placement5","rf_placement6","rf_placement7","rf_placement8","pid","contentID","moduletype","decisionType","clickURL","scenarioID","creativeGroupID","creativename","rf_placements","rf_bannerService","templateID"]
               },
                "liveRamp": {
                              "blackListKeywords": ["script", "embed", "object"],
                              "whiteListVariables": ["idl"]
               }             
}, // Security validation data for vendor integrations fetched from DB
		liveRampParseTempArray = []; // Temporary array to store the value when LiveRamp response is being parsed
	
	// JSON object variable to store the response messages for the new api LiveRamp integration	
	var liveRampMessage = {
			httpsFailure : "Https Failure - LiveRamp api doamin call encountered a https failure", // Exception message for the https failure scenario
			timedOut : "Timed Out - LiveRamp api doamin call is timed out", // Exception message for the call being timed out
			genericError : "Generic Error - Precise exception/failure for the api domain LiveRamp call is not found", // Precise exception/failure scenario being not caught
			timedOutHttpsMessage : "timeout", // Timeout text as received in the jqXHR object
			blackListValidationFailure : "Validtion Failure - Blacklisted Key found in response", // BlackList Key is found in LiveRamp new api domain response.
			whiteListValidationFailure : "Validtion Failure - Non whitelisted node is found in response", // Node in the response is not whitelisted
			parseFailure : "Parse Failure - The response received for parse is empty/null/undefined", // Response received to parse is empty/null/undefined
			success : "Success - Live Ramp new api domain integration is Success" // Live Ramp new api domain integration is Success 
		};	
		
	// JSON object variable to set indicator for  liveRamp call
	
	var liveRampIndicator = {
			callStatus: '-', // callStatus - check whether LiveRamp call success or error.  [1->(lr call success),0->(lr timedout/failed),- ->(no call)]
			idlResponse: '-', // idlResponse - set indicator depends upon response from LiveRamp call . 1->XY, 0->empty, 2->Xc, 3->Xi, - -> (no call)
			idlLinkInOS: '0', // idlLinkInOS - indicates if os request had idl value. 1->(idl in os), 0->(idl not in os)
			responseTime: '' // responseTime  - response time in ms for the LiveRamp call
	};
	
		
	(typeof liveRampFeatureOct18 != "undefined" && liveRampFeatureOct18) && triggerLiveRamp(); // invoke Liveramp function to trigger the Liveramp call for new api domain effective Oct 2018 release
	
	function prepareLiveRampUrl() { // Function to prepare the liveramp Url with query string params for new api domain implementation
		var liveRampUrl = liveRampUrl_newApi_Oct18; // Live Ramp Url fetched from the jfpglobal property
		liveRampUrl += "?pid=1&rt=idl"; // append the query string params to the live ramp base Url 
		return liveRampUrl; // return the dynamically formed liveramp Url to the requestor
	}

	function triggerLiveRamp() { // Function to trigger the liveramp new api domain

		$.ajax({
			url: prepareLiveRampUrl(),
			type: 'GET',
			start_time: new Date().getTime(),
			contentType: 'text/plain;charset=UTF-8',
			dataType: 'json',
			timeout: liveRampTimeout_newApi_Oct18,
			async: true,
			xhrFields: {
				withCredentials: true
			},
			success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) { // Function when Ajax Call is success
				liveRampIndicator.callStatus = '1';
				if (data && data.idl && data.idl!=undefined) {
					var lrResponse = data.idl.substring(0,2);
					liveRampIndicator.idlResponse = (lrResponse!='') ? ((lrResponse == 'XY') ? 1 : ((lrResponse == 'Xc') ? 2 : ((lrResponse == 'Xi') ? 3 : '-'))): '0';
				}else {
					liveRampIndicator.idlResponse = '0';
				}
				try {
					liveRampIndicator.responseTime = new Date().getTime() - this.start_time;
				} catch (e) {
					console.log('Error occurs in response time', e.message);
				}
				httpStatus = jqXHR.status || null;
				if (jqXHR.readyState == 4 ) { 
					(httpStatus >= 200 && httpStatus < 300) && (validateLiveRampResponse(JSON.stringify(data))); // Invoke validateLiveRampResponse function only if https code is between 200~300
				}
			},
			error: function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) { // Function when Ajax Call is error
				liveRampIndicator.callStatus = '0';
				try {
					liveRampIndicator.responseTime = new Date().getTime() - this.start_time;
				} catch (e) {
					console.log('Error occurs in response time', e.message);
				}
				httpStatus = jqXHR.status || null;
				if(textStatus == liveRampMessage.timedOutHttpsMessage) { // if the ajax status in jqXHR object is received as timeout
					updateLiveRampStatus("" , liveRampMessage.timedOut); // Update liveRampStatus variable failure node with timedOut status message
				}
				else {					
					if(isNaN(parseInt(httpStatus))) { // if https code of Ajax call is other than a number
						updateLiveRampStatus("" , liveRampMessage.genericError); // Update liveRampStatus variable failure node with generic error status message
					}
					else if(parseInt(httpStatus) >= 200 && parseInt(httpStatus) < 300) {
						updateLiveRampStatus("" , liveRampMessage.httpsFailure); // Update liveRampStatus variable failure node with https failure status message						
					}
					
				}
			},
			complete: function(jqXHR, textStatus) { // Function when Ajax Call is complete
					// Nothing to exectue post Live Ramp call response is parsed for idl value.
			}
		});
	}

	function validateLiveRampResponse(response) { // Function to validate the new api domain response for the live ramp integration
		
		var blackListKeywords = vendorData.liveRamp.blackListKeywords, // Fetch the black list keywords from vendorData
		 blackListKeyFound = false, // Set the flag to false for blackListmatch found
		 responseObject = JSON.parse(response); // Parse the response string and assign to the JSON response object

		// Blacklist validation of whole Live Ramp response
		for(var i = 0; i < blackListKeywords.length; i++) { // Iterate over for loop for the length of the blackList key words Array
			blackListKeyFound = (response.indexOf(blackListKeywords[i]) == -1) ? false : true; // Make boolean flag - blackListKeyFound to true when blackListKey is found in liveRamp response and vice versa 
			
			if(blackListKeyFound) {
				updateLiveRampStatus("", liveRampMessage.blackListValidationFailure);	// Update the failure node of liveRampStatus variable with blacklist validation failure message
				return;	// return from flow of validating the liveRamp response
			}
		}
		 
		 
		// White list validation of the keywords in the Live ramp response
		var whiteListKeys = vendorData.liveRamp.whiteListVariables, // Fetch the black list keywords from vendorData
			whitelistValidationFailure = false; // Set boolean whitelistValidationFailure flag to false before whitelist validation is started
		
		whiteListValidate(responseObject); // Invoke whiteListValidate function to perform whiteList validation
		
		function whiteListValidate(data) { // Implementation logic for the whitelist validation
			$.each(data, function(key, value) {
					if (($.inArray(key, liveRampParseTempArray) == -1) && !$.isArray(data))
						if (!$.isArray(data) && ($.inArray(key, whiteListKeys)==-1)) {	
							console.log("WhiteList Validation Failure - node not found in whitelist: " + key);			
							updateLiveRampStatus("", liveRampMessage.whiteListValidationFailure);
							whitelistValidationFailure = true;
							return;
						}	
			
				if (($.inArray(key, liveRampParseTempArray) == -1) && !$.isArray(data))
				liveRampParseTempArray.push(key);
				switch ($.type(value).toLowerCase()) {
						case "object":
							whiteListValidate(value);
							break;
				}
			});
		}
		(!whitelistValidationFailure) && (parseLiveRampResponse(response)); // Invoke parseLiveRampResponse function only if validation failure has not occured
	}
	
	function parseLiveRampResponse(response) {	// Function to parse the live ramp response to extract idl value
		if(response != "" && response != null && typeof response != "undefined") { // Validate the received response string for not being empty/null/undefined
			var responseObject = JSON.parse(response);	// JSON parse the string response
			(typeof responseObject.idl != "undefined" && responseObject.idl) ? (idl = responseObject.idl) : (idl = ""); // Validate the received idl value for not being null/undefined & assign global variable for idl with idl value from Live Ramp response
			(idl == "") ? (updateLiveRampStatus("", liveRampMessage.parseFailure)) : (updateLiveRampStatus("", liveRampMessage.success + "|" + idl)); // update liveRampStatus with parseFailure message (OR) success message as per execution
		}
	}

	function updateLiveRampStatus(successResponse, failureResponse) { // Function to update the liveRampStatus variable with the status of new api domain call for liveramp
		if(typeof successResponse != "undefined" && typeof failureResponse != "undefined") {
			liveRampStatus.success = successResponse; // Update the success node of the liveRampStatus
			liveRampStatus.failure = failureResponse; // Update the failure node of the liveRampStatus
		}
		else {
			liveRampStatus.success = ""; // Update the success node of the liveRampStatus with empty string as we received undefined in any of the argument params
			liveRampStatus.failure = liveRampStatus.updateStatusFailure; // Update the failure node of the liveRampStatus with exception message of update status failure message
		}
	}

</script>

<script>
function getParentLocation(){
return document.referrer;
}


	
function isSelfLoc(src){

	var result = false;
		
	/** parse out domain to make sure it points to our own **/
	if(src.substring(0, 7) == "http://" || src.substring(0, 8) == "https://") {
		var token = "://";
		var index = src.indexOf(token);
		var part = src.substring(index + token.length);
		var domain = "";
		
		/** parse up to end, first slash, or anchor **/
		for(var i=0; i<part.length; i++) {
			var character = part.charAt(i);
			
			if(character == '/' || character == ':' || character == '#') {
				break;
			} 
			else {
				domain += character;
			}
		}
		
		if(document.domain == domain){
			result=true;
		}		
	}
		
	return result;
}
	
function isXFSWhiteListed(parentLoc){   
	try {   
    	var result=false;
    	var XFSWhitelist="";
    	
    	if(XFSWhitelist.toLowerCase() == "null" || XFSWhitelist == "" || XFSWhitelist.length==0 ){
		    return false;
	    }
		if(parentLoc.toLowerCase() == "null" || parentLoc== "" || parentLoc.length==0 ){
		    return false;
	    }

	    if(isSelfLoc(parentLoc)){
		    return true;
	    }
	    
		var allowedLocations=XFSWhitelist.split("||");
		var allowedDomains = allowedLocations[0].split(" ");
		var isDomainAllowed = false;
		for (index = 0; index < allowedDomains.length; index++) {
			var token = "://";
			var pos = parentLoc.indexOf(token);
			var prefix=parentLoc.substring(0,pos+token.length);
			var part = parentLoc.substring(pos + token.length);
			var parentDomain = "";
			for(var i=0; i<part.length; i++) {
				var character = part.charAt(i);

				if(character == '/' || character == '#') {
					break;
				} else {
					parentDomain += character;
				}
			}

		parentDomain=prefix+parentDomain;
		if (parentDomain== (allowedDomains[index])) {
				isDomainAllowed = true;
				break;
			} 
		}
		
		if (isDomainAllowed){
			if(allowedLocations[1] == "*"){
				result=true;
			}
			else {  
				var allowedPages = allowedLocations[1].split("^");
				for (index = 0; index < allowedPages.length; ++index) {
					if(parentLoc.contains(allowedPages[index]) ) {
						result = true;
					}
				}
			}          
		}			
		return result;	   
    }   
    catch (err) {   
		return false;   
    }   
}  	

</script>

		<noscript>
		
		
		
		<STYLE TYPE='text/css'>
		body {display:none;visibility:hidden;}
		</STYLE>
		
		
		
		</noscript>
		
		<style>
			html {  display:none;visibility:hidden; }
		</style>

		var parentLocation = getParentLocation();
   	  var XFSWhitelisted= isXFSWhiteListed(parentLocation);
			if(  self == top || XFSWhitelisted ){
				
	   	 		 document.documentElement.style.display ='block';
				document.documentElement.style.visibility='visible';
				
			}else{
				top.location = self.location;
			}
		</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
String.prototype.startsWith = function(prefix) {
		return this.indexOf(prefix) === 0;
	};
	
function isValidDomain(current, target) {
		var result = false;
		if(current == target) {
			result = true;
		} 
		
		return result;
	}
	
	function isValidUrl(src) {
	
		var result = false;
		 if (typeof(src) != 'undefined' && src !== null) {
		if(src.substring(0, 7) == "http://" || src.substring(0, 8) == "https://") {
			var token = "://";
			var index = src.indexOf(token);
			var part = src.substring(index + token.length);
			var domain = "";
			for(var i=0; i<part.length; i++) {
				var character = part.charAt(i);

				if(character == '/' || character == ':' || character == '#') {
					break;
				} else {
					domain += character;
				}
			}
			
			result = isValidDomain(document.domain, domain);
		
		} else if(src.charAt(0) == '#') {
			result = false;
		} else if(!src.startsWith("//") && (src.charAt(0) == '/' || src.indexOf(':') == -1)) {
			result = true;
		}
		}
		else{
		result=true;
		}
		return result;
	}
	
		


</script>

<script>
function getParentLocation(){
return document.referrer;
}


	
function isSelfLoc(src){

	var result = false;
		
	/** parse out domain to make sure it points to our own **/
	if(src.substring(0, 7) == "http://" || src.substring(0, 8) == "https://") {
		var token = "://";
		var index = src.indexOf(token);
		var part = src.substring(index + token.length);
		var domain = "";
		
		/** parse up to end, first slash, or anchor **/
		for(var i=0; i<part.length; i++) {
			var character = part.charAt(i);
			
			if(character == '/' || character == ':' || character == '#') {
				break;
			} 
			else {
				domain += character;
			}
		}
		
		if(document.domain == domain){
			result=true;
		}		
	}
		
	return result;
}
	
function isXFSWhiteListed(parentLoc){   
	try {   
    	var result=false;
    	var XFSWhitelist="";
    	
    	if(XFSWhitelist.toLowerCase() == "null" || XFSWhitelist == "" || XFSWhitelist.length==0 ){
		    return false;
	    }
		if(parentLoc.toLowerCase() == "null" || parentLoc== "" || parentLoc.length==0 ){
		    return false;
	    }

	    if(isSelfLoc(parentLoc)){
		    return true;
	    }
	    
		var allowedLocations=XFSWhitelist.split("||");
		var allowedDomains = allowedLocations[0].split(" ");
		var isDomainAllowed = false;
		for (index = 0; index < allowedDomains.length; index++) {
			var token = "://";
			var pos = parentLoc.indexOf(token);
			var prefix=parentLoc.substring(0,pos+token.length);
			var part = parentLoc.substring(pos + token.length);
			var parentDomain = "";
			for(var i=0; i<part.length; i++) {
				var character = part.charAt(i);

				if(character == '/' || character == '#') {
					break;
				} else {
					parentDomain += character;
				}
			}

		parentDomain=prefix+parentDomain;
		if (parentDomain== (allowedDomains[index])) {
				isDomainAllowed = true;
				break;
			} 
		}
		
		if (isDomainAllowed){
			if(allowedLocations[1] == "*"){
				result=true;
			}
			else {  
				var allowedPages = allowedLocations[1].split("^");
				for (index = 0; index < allowedPages.length; ++index) {
					if(parentLoc.contains(allowedPages[index]) ) {
						result = true;
					}
				}
			}          
		}			
		return result;	   
    }   
    catch (err) {   
		return false;   
    }   
}  	

</script>

	<style>
		html {display:none;visibility:hidden; }
	</style>
	<script>
		
		try {
			var parentLocation = getParentLocation();
		 	var XFSWhitelisted= isXFSWhiteListed(parentLocation);
		  	var topDM = top.document.domain;
		
		  if(topDM == document.domain || XFSWhitelisted ){
		  document.documentElement.style.display ='block';
		  	document.documentElement.style.visibility='visible';
		  }else{
		  	top.location = self.location;
		  }
		}
		catch (e) {
			top.location = self.location;
		}

		
		
	</script>

			function ngaKA() {
				var cookieName = "NGACoExistenceCookie";
				if(getCookie(cookieName)) {
					//can set to retrieve value for the interval from cookie if needed
					var intrVl = 620;
					if(isNaN(intrVl)){
						intrVl=620;
					}
					intrVl *= 1000;
					var contextPathNGA = "/US";

			       /* if (( contextPathNGA === undefined ) || ( contextPathNGA == null ) || ( contextPathNGA == "undefined" ) || ( contextPathNGA == "" )){
			                contextPathNGA = contextPath;
			        }

			        if (( contextPathNGA === undefined ) || ( contextPathNGA == null ) || ( contextPathNGA == "undefined" ) || ( contextPathNGA == "" )){
			                contextPathNGA = "/US";
			        }*/
					
					var urlNGA = contextPathNGA + "/NGA/coext/CThreeKA.do";	
					$.ajax({
						type: "GET",
						url: urlNGA,
						complete: function() {
							//can set to retrieve value for the interval from cookie if needed
							//var exTime = 5;
							//var exdate = new Date();
							//exdate.setMinutes(exdate.getMinutes() + exTime);
							//var expires = "expires="+ exdate.toUTCString();
							//var c_value = getCookie("NGACoExistenceCookie");
							//document.cookie = cookieName + "=" + c_value + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
							setTimeout(ngaKA, intrVl);
						}
					});
				}
			}
			function getCookie(name)
			{
				var c=""+document.cookie;
				var index = c.indexOf(name + "=");
				if (index == -1) return null;
				var endstr = c.indexOf(";", index);
				if (endstr == -1) endstr = c.length;
				return unescape(c.substring(index+name.length+1, endstr));
			}

var PRConfig = {
PRURL: "//ui.powerreviews.com/stable/4.0/ui.js",

<script>
	var PRcallback;

	function reviewsClicked(cardURL){
		window.open(cardURL,"_self");
	}
	
	 function prConnection(callback,e) {
		var loadScript = function (callback) {
			jQuery.ajax({
				url: PRConfig.PRURL,
				dataType: 'script',
				success: callback,
				async: true
			});
		}
	 
		if (typeof POWERREVIEWS == 'undefined') {
			loadScript(callback);
		} else {
			callback();
		}
		
		// Dynamically adding href attribute to open cards landing page in new tab if right clicked and selected open in new tab option.
		setTimeout(function(){
			$('div.pr-snippet-read-and-write a.pr-snippet-review-count').attr('href',e.ctaLink); 
		},3000);	
	 }
         
	 function setReview_banner(PID, components, readClick) {

		if(typeof readClick == 'undefined'){
			PRcallback = '';
		}else{
			PRcallback = function(){
					reviewsClicked(readClick);
				};
		}
		return {
			api_key: PRConfig.PRAPIKey,
			locale: 'en_US',
			merchant_group_id: PRConfig.PRMerchantGrpId,
			merchant_id: PRConfig.PRMerchantId,
			page_id: PID,
			review_wrapper_url: '../standalone.4.0.html?pageId=~~~PAGE_ID~~~',
			components: components,
			on_read_reviews_click:PRcallback,
		};
	 }
         
	 function fetchPRReviews(e) {
		var self = this;
		var items = self.setReview_banner(e.pid, {ReviewSnippet: 'prstars'},e.ctaLink);
	 
		this.prConnection(function () {
			POWERREVIEWS.display.render(items);
		},e);
	 }
	 
</script>

	jQuery(document).ready(function() {
		var currDate = new Date();
		var expiry = new Date(currDate .getTime() +1000*60*60*24*365).toUTCString();
		
		/* count cookie is to count the total number of hit. If count cookie is not present create it */
		
		if(document.cookie.indexOf("count") == -1){
			document.cookie = "count=0;expires="+expiry +";path=/";
		}
			var cookies = document.cookie;
			//if count cookie is present then get the value and increament by 1 for each page load and display migrated user alert untill 3
			if(cookies.indexOf("count") != -1){
				var cookieVal = parseInt(getCookie("count")) +1;
				setCookie("count",cookieVal,expiry);
				if(getCookie("count") <= 3){
				window.migratedAlert="true";
					}
		 }
		 
		
		//if spanish page then display translation alert
		if(language.indexOf('es_') != -1){
			window.translationAlert = "true"
		}
		// if alert does not display then adjust the hero module placement for first timer
		if($('#alert-block').is(':hidden')){
			$("div.heroContainer").addClass("adjustHeroMod");
		}
		//Alert US ends
		// removing to unmask the userid
		/* doMask(); */ 
		
		

		if($('#alert-block').is(':hidden')){
			$(".signonContainer").addClass("top80");
			//$("div.heroContainer").removeClass("adjustHeroModMobile");
		}
		//$("div.heroContainer").removeClass("adjustHeroModMobile");

		if('[]' != undefined && '[]'.length > 2){
				detachedRemChkBoxDesktop = $("#rememberBlockDesktop .rememberBlock").detach();
				detachedRemChkBoxMobile = $("#rememberBlockMobile .rememberBlock").detach();
				/* hero and signon module swaping in small screens */
				//$("#desktop-only").addClass("hidden-sm hidden-xs");
				//$("section.sign-on-module").addClass("top80");
				if($('#alert-block').is(':hidden')){
					$(".signonContainer").addClass("top80");
				}
				
					$("div.cookiedHero").addClass("topZero");
				
		}
		
			// if cookied and alert is not there then adjust the signon module and hero module
			
	
	 	/* uncheck the checkbox on page load */
		$("input[type='checkbox']").prop('checked', false);
		/* select the first option when coming to homepage after clicking back btn */
		$("#cookiedList").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
		
		$("#usernameMasked").attr("placeholder",maskedPlaceHolder);
		$("#usernameMasked").attr("aria-hidden", false);
		$("#usernameMasked").attr("aria-label","User ID");
		
		
		//private browsing alert 
		try{
			sessionStorage.setItem("test","1");
			sessionStorage.removeItem("test");
		} catch(e){
			(typeof privateBrowserAlert != "undefined") && $("#privateBrowserAlert").modal({backdrop:'static',keyboard:false});
		}
		
		//initMLC();
		var year=$("#br_year, .br_year");
		if(year.length > 0 && year.html()=="") 
		year.html((new Date()).getFullYear());

		 if(true){
				$.ajax({
					url:iovationUrl,
					dataType: "script", 
					complete:function(){
					removeSignonLock();
					if (callbackFunction != undefined){
						callbackFunction();
						callbackFunction=null;
						}
					}
				});
				setTimeout ( function () {
					removeSignonLock();
					if (callbackFunction != undefined){
						callbackFunction();
						callbackFunction=null;
					}
				}, 3000 );
				}
	 	 }
	 	 /*alert*/
		
		for (var i = 0; i < alerts.alertData.length; i++) {
			var thisAlertData = alerts.alertData[i];
			if(window.browserAlert == "true" && thisAlertData.alertType == "browser-alert"){
				passTmplObj(thisAlertData);
			}else if(window.migratedAlert == "true" && thisAlertData.alertType == "migration-alert"){
				passTmplObj(thisAlertData);
			}else if(thisAlertData.alertType == "relevant-alert"){
				passTmplObj(thisAlertData);
			} else if(window.translationAlert == "true" && thisAlertData.alertType == "translation-alert"){
				passTmplObj(thisAlertData);			
			} else if(thisAlertData.alertType == "outage-alert"){
				passTmplObj(thisAlertData);	
			} else if(thisAlertData.alertType == "weather-alert"){
				passTmplObj(thisAlertData);
			}
		}
	
		$("div.alertSection").on("click", ".showCTA", function(e){
			var targetEl = e.target.id;
			showAlerts(targetEl );
			
		});
		$("div.alertSection").on("keydown", ".showCTA", function(e){
			if(e.keyCode == 13){
				var targetEl = e.target.id;
				showAlerts(targetEl );
			}
		});

	
		$("div.alertSection").on("click", ".hideCTA", function(e){
			var targetEl = e.target.id;
			hideAlerts(targetEl);
			
		});

				hideAlerts(targetEl);
			}	
		});

		handleOutageAlert(alerts);

	<script type="text/javascript">
	var signonLock = true;
	var callbackFunction;
	
	     
	var io_install_flash = false;  
	var io_install_stm = false; 
	var io_bbout_element_id = 'ioBlackBox'; 
	var io_exclude_stm = 12;
	var iovationUrl = "https://mpsnare.iesnare.com/snare.js";
	var iovationTimeout = '3000';
	var iovationNotAvailable='';

	function setIOBlackBox(myForm){  
		if(myForm.ioBlackBox !=null && myForm.ioBlackBox != 'undefined')
		{
			myForm.ioBlackBox.value = deviceprint_blackbox(); 
		}
	}
	function deviceprint_blackbox()
	{
		if ((typeof ioGetBlackbox) != "undefined"){
			var bb_data = ioGetBlackbox();
			if ( bb_data) {
				var ioBlackBox = bb_data.blackbox;
				return ioBlackBox;
			}
		} else {
			return iovationNotAvailable;
		}
	}	
	function removeSignonLock(){
		signonLock=false;
	}	
	</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
var targetElement; //fix for defect #6062
$("a.speedBump").on("click", function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			targetElement = $(this); //fix for defect #6062
			setTimeout(function(){
				openlink(e);
			},200)
		});
		function openlink(e){
	      	var rel;
			var el = $(e.target);
        	if (el.is("a")){
					e.preventDefault();
					window.rel = el.attr('href');
        	}   
        	else{
            		window.rel = el.parent().attr('href');
       		}
			$('#speedBumpModal').modal({backdrop: 'true', keyboard: false}) ;
		}		
		$("#overlayBtn").on("click", function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			OpenInNewTab(rel);
			$("#speedBumpModal").modal('hide');
			$(targetElement).focus(); //fix for defect #6062
		});
		//fix for defect #6062
		$("#speedBumpModal button.close").on("click", function(){
			$("#speedBumpModal").modal('hide');
			$(targetElement).focus(); 
		});
		
		/* Accordion menu fix */
		$('.accordion').each(function() {
        	var accordion = new CM.Accordion(this);
        	accordion.init();
    	});
});

function OpenInNewTab(url) {
	  var win = window.open(url, '_blank');
	  win.focus();
}
</script>

<script>
function firstCobrowseOverlay() {
	hideOverlay();
	if($("div#bodyWrapper.cbolui-ddl").length == 0
			&& $("div.cbolui-ddl-pre").length == 0) {
		if (jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget != undefined) {
		  jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget('open');
		} else {
			console.log("showing manualCobrowseOverlay");
			$('#manualCobrowseOverlay').css("display","block");
		}
		  jQuery(".snumber").val("").focus();
		  
		} else {
			if ($('div.DDLCobrowseOverlay').css('display') == "none") {
				$('div.DDLCobrowseOverlay').css({'display':'inline'});
			}
			$("#cobrowseModalWithTextInput").modal('show');
			$('.DDLCobrowseOverlay').css("visibility","visible"); 
			$('.modal-backdrop.fade').css("visibility","visible"); 
			$('.modal-backdrop.fade.in').css("visibility","visible");
		}
}

function hideOverlay() {
	if($("div#bodyWrapper.cbolui-ddl").length != 0
			|| $("div.cbolui-ddl-pre").length != 0) { 
		$('.DDLCobrowseOverlay').css("visibility","hidden"); 
		$('.modal-backdrop.fade').css("visibility","hidden"); 
		$('.modal-backdrop.fade.in').css("visibility","hidden");
	} else {
		if (jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget != undefined) {
			jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget('close');
		} else { 
			$('#manualCobrowseOverlay').css("display","none");
		}
	}
	
}

function cobrowseOverlay(){
	if($("div#bodyWrapper.cbolui-ddl").length == 0
			&& $("div.cbolui-ddl-pre").length == 0) {
		if (jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget != undefined) {
		  jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget('open');
		} else {
			$('#manualCobrowseOverlay').css("display","block");
		}
		  jQuery(".snumber").val("").focus();
		  
		} else {
			$('.DDLCobrowseOverlay').css("visibility","visible"); 
			$('.modal-backdrop.fade').css("visibility","visible"); 
			$('.modal-backdrop.fade.in').css("visibility","visible");	
		}
}

function showAlert(invalid) {
	var alertmsg;
	if (invalid == '1') {
		if (_locale.indexOf('es_US') == 0) {
			alertmsg = "El nmero de servicio no es vlido";
		} else {
			alertmsg = "The service number is invalid";
		}
	} else {
		if (_locale.indexOf('es_US') == 0) {
			alertmsg = "Por favor ingrese el nmero de servicio";
		} else {
			alertmsg = "Please enter service number";
		}
	}
	alert(alertmsg);
}

setTimeout(function() {
jQuery("#cobrowseModalWithTextInput button.btn.btn-primary").click(function() {
	  var serviceId;
	    if (jQuery("#i51").length == 2) {
	        serviceId = jQuery("#i51:eq(1)").val();
	            //alert(serviceId);
	    } else {
	        serviceId = jQuery("#i51").val();
	            //alert(serviceId);
	   }
	    if (serviceId) {
	    	hideOverlay();
	        requestCobrowse(serviceId);
	    }
		
		if (jQuery("#i51").length !== 2 && jQuery("#i51").val() == "") {
			showAlert(0);

	} else if (jQuery("#i51:eq(1)").val() == "") {
		showAlert(0);

	} else {
	}
		
});

$('#co-browse').keypress(function(event){
	if (event.which == 13) {
		firstCobrowseOverlay();
	}
});

jQuery("#co-browse").click(function() {
	firstCobrowseOverlay();
});

jQuery(".cancelbtn").click(function() {
	if (jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget != undefined) {
		jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget('close');
	} else {
		$('#manualCobrowseOverlay').css("display","none");
	}
});

jQuery(document).off('click', '#cobrowseDialogueBox .okbtn').on('click', '#cobrowseDialogueBox .okbtn',function(e) {
    var serviceId = jQuery("#cobrowseDialogueBox .snumber").val();
    if (serviceId) {   
    	jQuery('#cobrowseDialogueBox').jfpwidget('close');
        requestCobrowse(serviceId);
    } else {
    	showAlert(0);
        cobrowseOverlay();
    }
});

jQuery(document).off('click', '#manualCobrowseOverlay .okbtn').on('click', '#manualCobrowseOverlay .okbtn',function(e) {
    var serviceId = jQuery("#manualCobrowseOverlay .snumber").val();
    if (serviceId) {
       	$('#manualCobrowseOverlay').css("display","none");
        requestCobrowse(serviceId);
    } else {
    	showAlert(0);
        cobrowseOverlay();
    }
});
}, 1);

/**
* Requests a CoBrowse session using an agent's service id. This can be used in phone-only scenarios when
* CoBrowse cannot be started via chat.
*
* Example Usage: requestCobrowse("123456");
* @param serviceId
*/
function requestCobrowse(serviceId) {
	lpTag.taglets.cobrowse.loadApi(function (visitorApi) {
		console.log("CoBrowse visitor API loaded");
		visitorApi.once("sessionRejected", function () {
			showAlert(1);
			cobrowseOverlay();
		});
		visitorApi.once("sessionOffered", function (event) {
			console.log("Agent answered the request and offers a CoBrowse session");
			
			/*Site catalyst tracking begin*/
			citiData.pageName="co-browse overlay";
			citiData.custLink="share your screen success";
			citiData.customLinkClick ="CoBrowseEvent";
			Bootstrapper.ensEvent.trigger("customLinkClick");
			/*site catalyst tracking end*/
			
			var automaticallyAcceptOffer = true; // Set to false if you would like to ask the visitor to confirm the session start.
			
			if (automaticallyAcceptOffer || confirm("Would you like to start a CoBrowse session with '" + event.agentAlias + "'?")) {
			visitorApi.acceptSupportOffer(event);
			} else {
			visitorApi.cancelSupportOffer(event);
			}
		});
	
		function sessionReadyCallback(startEvent) {
			if (startEvent) {
			console.log("Session is ready and will be started shortly.");
			}
		}
		visitorApi.requestSupport({serviceId: serviceId}, sessionReadyCallback);
	});
}

</script>
